===== 문제 1 =====
유형: 문장형
질문: Which of the following procedures is correct when applying for a mobile driver’s license?
① Applications can be made using any app.
② Applications must be made using a smartphone under the applicant’s name with identity verification.
③ Applications can only be made at the traffic civil service office of a police station.
④ A mobile driver’s license cannot be issued at a driver’s license test center.
정답: 2

④ 4 years
